# 🗂️ ULTRA WORKSPACE STRUCTURE MAP

📅 Generated: 2025-06-10 (Updated)
📁 Root: /root/chaosgenius

## 🗺️ LEGENDARY WORKSPACE MAP LEGEND

### 📂 **DIRECTORY SYMBOLS**

- 🏠 `./` - Root directory (home base)
- 📁 `folder/` - Standard directory/folder
- 📂 `special/` - Important system directory

### 📄 **FILE TYPE ICONS**

- 🐍 `.py` - Python files (core system files)
- 📄 `.txt, .cfg, .ini` - Configuration & text files
- 📝 `.md` - Markdown documentation files
- 🗃️ `.db, .sqlite` - Database files
- ⚡ `.sh` - Shell scripts (executable)
- 💛 `.js` - JavaScript files
- 📊 `.json` - JSON configuration/data files
- 🎨 `.html, .css` - Web frontend files
- 🖼️ `.svg, .png` - Graphics & image files
- 🔧 `.yml, .yaml` - YAML configuration files
- 📦 `.tar.gz, .zip` - Compressed archives
- 🧪 `test_*.py` - Test files
- 🔒 `.env` - Environment variables (secrets)
- 🖥️ `.ps1` - PowerShell scripts
- 🗄️ `.deb` - Debian packages
- 📋 `.ipynb` - Jupyter Notebooks
- 🖼️ `.desktop` - Linux desktop files
- 🎯 `.service` - System service files
- 🔗 `.workspace` - VS Code workspace files

### 📏 **SIZE INDICATORS**

- `(25B)` - Bytes (tiny files)
- `(1KB)` - Kilobytes (small files)
- `(10KB)` - Medium files
- `(1MB)` - Large files
- `(37MB)` - Huge files (like IPFS Kubo)

### 🎯 **SPECIAL MARKERS**

- `✅` - Active/working features
- `🔥` - Hot/frequently used
- `⭐` - Core system files
- `🚀` - Deployment related
- `🛡️` - Security components
- `🧠` - AI/ML components
- `💰` - Revenue/business related
- `🌐` - Web3/IPFS related
- `👥` - Community features
- `🌀` - Ultra/Special edition components
- `🎮` - Gaming/Gamification features
- `📱` - Mobile components
- `⚡` - Performance optimized

### 📊 **PROJECT CATEGORIES**

#### 🎯 **CORE SYSTEM**

- Main application files (`app.py`, `broski_core.py`)
- Core business logic
- Database connections
- API endpoints (`api/`, `dashboard_api.py`)

- HTML dashboards (`frontend/`, `*.html`)

- Web assets (`static/`, `assets/`)
- Portal interfaces (`*_portal.html`)

#### 🌍 **WEB3 & IPFS**

- Blockchain integration
- Decentralized hosting
- Kubo node files

#### 🏭 **PRODUCTION READY**

- Deployment configs (`production_config/`, `deploy/`)
- Environment setups (`*_env/`)

- Monitoring tools (`*_monitor.py`)

### 🔧 **NAMING CONVENTIONS**

#### **VERSION SUFFIXES**

- `_1_1_1.py` - Version 1.1.1

- `broski_*` - BROski system components

- `agent_*` - AI agent files

- `*_docs/` - Documentation folders
